GT Equivalence Verification (CRK17)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_f*A**c3
Candidate formulas: 77

GT is the fixed function
\[
F(t,A)=0.2084703204063362\,A^{1/3}\;-\;0.6750544468008356\,A\,e^{-0.0783132263146032\,t}.
\]
So any matching candidate must be exactly “(constant)\(\cdot A^{1/3}\) + (constant)\(\cdot A e^{(constant)\,t}\)” with **no other surviving dependence on \(t\) or \(A\)**.

Below, for each candidate, I check whether extra terms can be eliminated by setting candidate constants to 0, and whether the remaining terms can be parameter-set to the GT coefficients/exponent.

---

### 1.
Has extra log/Abs/sin/cos term. Set \(c3=0\) to remove it → reduces to \(A^{1/3}c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t}\), which can match GT by choosing \(c0=0.2084703\), \(c1=-0.6750544\), \(c2=-0.0783132\). **Matches.**

### 2.
Contains \(A^{1/3}c1 e^{A c2}\sin(\cdot)\) which depends on \(A\) inside exp and trig; must vanish: set \(c1=0\). Then left with \(A^{1/3}c0 + A c5 e^{c6 t}\) → can match with \(c0=0.2084703\), \(c5=-0.6750544\), \(c6=-0.0783132\). **Matches.**

### 3.
Already \(A^{1/3}c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t}\). Choose \(c0=0.2084703\), \(c1=-0.6750544\), \(c2=-0.0783132\). **Matches.**

### 4.
Extra rational-in-\(|A|\) term; set \(c3=0\) to remove. Remaining matches as in (3). **Matches.**

### 5.
Extra sine term; set \(c3=0\). Remaining matches as in (3). **Matches.**

### 6.
Extra \(\frac{A c3}{c4 t+c5}+\frac{c6}{c4 t+c5}\); set \(c3=0,c6=0\). Remaining matches as in (3). **Matches.**

### 7.
Extra \(\;c3 |A|/(c4+|A|)^2\); set \(c3=0\). Remaining matches as in (3). **Matches.**

### 8.
Extra constant \(c3\) and log term; set \(c3=0,c4=0\). Remaining matches as in (3). **Matches.**

### 9.
Form \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 |A|^{c3}\).
To match GT, the second term must become \(0.20847 A^{1/3}\), but it is \(A\cdot |A|^{c3}\), i.e. scales like \(|A|^{c3+1}\) (and has sign issues for \(A<0\)). You could set \(c2=0\) to remove it, but then you lose the \(A^{1/3}\) term. **Cannot match.**

### 10.
